        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1104748646" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16397346107768447337"><b>5 Blow me Away Stars*****</b><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/BD517866-2C02-4B26-8BDD-6004364B4B2D_zpsqaybyo5o.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416396101i/11952350._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo BD517866-2C02-4B26-8BDD-6004364B4B2D_zpsqaybyo5o.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a> <br/><br/><br/>Wow just wow, I read a lot of erotica and to be honest its not always out of choice but you know I kind of end up falling into those reads which I love but recently I was in the need to a NA college romance/Sports Romance I mean this is one of my go to reads when I want to go back to college to remember KWIM?? I'm a 34 wife/mum so its not something I read all the time just occasionally saying that, please don't judge this book by its cover which I kind of of did a f</span>
  <span id="freeText16397346107768447337" style="display:none"><b>5 Blow me Away Stars*****</b><br><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/BD517866-2C02-4B26-8BDD-6004364B4B2D_zpsqaybyo5o.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416396101i/11952350._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo BD517866-2C02-4B26-8BDD-6004364B4B2D_zpsqaybyo5o.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br><br>Wow just wow, I read a lot of erotica and to be honest its not always out of choice but you know I kind of end up falling into those reads which I love but recently I was in the need to a NA college romance/Sports Romance I mean this is one of my go to reads when I want to go back to college to remember KWIM?? I'm a 34 wife/mum so its not something I read all the time just occasionally saying that, please don't judge this book by its cover which I kind of of did a few months back when I first cast my eyes on it but hey I was in the need of a sports romance themed story and bam here I am blown away by this book, the words and thoughts of these characters were just so mature I honestly was hooked from page one. <br> <br>Anyway I digress... <br> <br>drews Mum once told him that...<br><b>
  <blockquote>Life, She insisted, is how you live it and who you live it with, not what you do to make a living.</blockquote>
</b><br> <br>And....<br> <b>
  <blockquote>"You'll see, Drew. One day, Love will creep up and smack you upside the head. Then you'll understand."</blockquote>
</b> <br> <br>You see Drew is a football player he is the main one, the one everyone wants to see the <b>'ONE' </b>everyone wants. But hey that doesn't mean he's happy, then one day he see's one girl this girl namely Anna Jones is then ALL he see's but she's a nothing in her eyes, a small fish in a big pond concerning Drew in her eyes. Here we have two people who are moving forward in their lives but not necessarily enjoying what they have cause they have a big whole to fill. <br><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/FE2BAFAB-07CF-4289-827E-72FD1F46662E_zpsj3ulban7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416396101i/11952351._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo FE2BAFAB-07CF-4289-827E-72FD1F46662E_zpsj3ulban7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>Drew has his team and he's happy he works extremely hard, he trains he plays and he studies but he doesn't drink and he watches out for his boys so when his eyes meet Anna HE WANTS HER FOR HIM. <br><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/6FA6501E-BA6D-481C-8BBD-24CF31916A0D_zpsijblvlaq.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416396101i/11952352._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 6FA6501E-BA6D-481C-8BBD-24CF31916A0D_zpsijblvlaq.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>You know there's that moment when you need and want its definitely the case for Drew the only thing is Anna rebels and may want him back but won't admit it so there are rules and they go like this:<br> <br><b>no kissing on the mouth, no staying the night, no telling anyone, and above all… No falling in love.</b><br> <br>So can Drew break that rule and turn Anna around to his thinking?? <br> <br>Anna Jones doesn't know what she wants to do with her life she's at college and all but the only thing she would like is to be in New York, She lives with her friend and enjoys her little life of contentment studying, working but after a not great break up in her past she doesn't do relationships she doesn't want the feelings that go with it nor has she been out recently that is until her friends get her out where she bumps into Drew and where they start their Hook Up now I'm not going to tell you much more about the story just lets say emotions obviously get involved and its time to take a chance when you just know right??<br><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/4C184552-61A9-4F2F-80D9-3B9E2AF2C161_zpsmxuxfmux.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416179535i/11907898._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 4C184552-61A9-4F2F-80D9-3B9E2AF2C161_zpsmxuxfmux.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br><b>My thoughts</b><br>Here I am sitting trying the fathom the right words to express how much joy this book gave me, its has the sweet romance and getting to know you feel and then there's the whole I NEED YOU NOW feel, friendship, love and sex its all there, there chemisty was off the charts and majority of this read I was panting in my seat and wondering whats going to happen next I never got bored of it too, really this NA was not inappropriate or unrealistic the maturity of the story gripped me and I was thinking about it throughout the day which to means a good story to me. <br><br>I loved how it was a gradual process I say mature again cause this really is a <b>LOVE STORY TO ITS CORE</b><br><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/926E649B-C5EA-4969-92B4-B4E81FA57581_zpsutoxe2ju.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416396101i/11952353._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 926E649B-C5EA-4969-92B4-B4E81FA57581_zpsutoxe2ju.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>I was asked yesterday if this story was generic and I suppose yes it is but please don't let that put you off, I enjoyed it for what it is don't expect lots of plot twists but if your in the mood then please grab it.<br><br><b>To Sum Up</b><br>The author did a great job at building the tension at the beginning and making me smile at the end Job well done Kristen I'll be awaiting for Grays book coming next..... <br><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/69F99236-3290-4121-8507-45DFEDEE35DD_zpsuxj0jjbc.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416396101i/11952354._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 69F99236-3290-4121-8507-45DFEDEE35DD_zpsuxj0jjbc.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br> <br>Read it, that is all..... <br> </span>

<div id="review_1434341647" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1434341647" />
    <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy"><img alt="Stacey is Sassy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1474185067p2/12062194.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1434341647?book_show_action=true">Nov 05, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacey is Sassy" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy">Stacey is Sassy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23171970-the-hook-up">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=favourites-2015">favourites-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=cont-sports">cont-sports</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=cont-series">cont-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1434341647" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16886170602028251330"><strong>These bloody good NA books are making a liar out of me.</strong><br/><br/>I'm pretty sure my profile on Goodreads says something along the lines of - NA are not for me. The Hook Up proved me wrong. I AM into books that suck me in, make me laugh, blush, cry and grumble, teach me something (how's that headache Sparkles?) and leaves me with a big smile on my face. New Adult books seem to have turned a corner. We are not bombarded with chicks who lose their mental capacity because they want a certain blokes attention.</span>
  <span id="freeText16886170602028251330" style="display:none"><strong>These bloody good NA books are making a liar out of me.</strong><br><br>I'm pretty sure my profile on Goodreads says something along the lines of - NA are not for me. The Hook Up proved me wrong. I AM into books that suck me in, make me laugh, blush, cry and grumble, teach me something (how's that headache Sparkles?) and leaves me with a big smile on my face. New Adult books seem to have turned a corner. We are not bombarded with chicks who lose their mental capacity because they want a certain blokes attention. It's not just assumed that a guy ONLY thinks with his bits and pieces. This book grabbed my attention with characters that have goals and work bloody hard to reach them and feel satisfaction when their hard work pays off.<br><br>Big Red...what was Drew thinking? I cringed as soon as I read the words. He certainly picked the wrong girl to say it to. Anna, is not afraid to put Drew in his place when he assumes she'd jump at the chance to be with him. After all he is the star quarterback and practically famous. Neither of them can deny their overwhelming attraction to each other, but while Drew is keen, Anna is friggin petrified. Both Anna and Drew have reasons for their eagerness and hesitations. We see their relationship stutter and start from the beginning to the end. Both of them are not as confident as they would have everyone believe.<br><br>I loved the characters in this story, especially with Anna and Drew's friends playing pivotal roles. There were some deeper issues dealt with that made it seem more realistic. I also liked the way the author showed Drew's reaction, to someone else's reaction, to being on the receiving end of a 6 ft 4 muscle bound man who's angry. More times than not he cools his jets to make sure they don't feel threatened. Nice to see a football player portrayed with intelligence, control and sensitivity.<br><br>I'm still not ready to call myself a NA fan, but with this caliber of work, I can't help but be a little keen to try some more. This was my first book by Kristen Callihan and with that much talent, it will definitely not be my last.<br><br>To buy The Hook Up from Amazon - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1Q6M1E0">http://amzn.to/1Q6M1E0</a><br><br><a href="http://staceyissassy.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440643271i/16004133._SX540_.jpg" width="300" height="48" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/Sassyreviews" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440644070i/16004243.jpg" width="40" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="https://www.pinterest.com/Stacey1565/" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440644070i/16004244.jpg" width="40" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="https://www.twitter.com/StaceyisSassy" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440644070i/16004245.jpg" width="40" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a></a></span>

    <a title="Beverly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly"><img alt="Beverly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466964369p2/13095060.jpg" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beverly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beverly" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly">Beverly</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1053046004" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14785173706052332952"><b>Perfectly sweet, perfectly sexy and perfectly addictive! </b> Drew Baylor is the star quarterback on a winning football team. I am from the South where footballs king, so I totally understood the allure of Drew. The star football player on a winning football team is everything here, and <i>Battle Baylor</i> is everything there too.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452132102i/17650873._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Naturally Anna assumes Drew is just like every other jock, perhaps even worse since he is the star quarterback. Anna decides her and Drew can hook up, but she won’t offer him any</span>
  <span id="freeText14785173706052332952" style="display:none"><b>Perfectly sweet, perfectly sexy and perfectly addictive! </b> Drew Baylor is the star quarterback on a winning football team. I am from the South where footballs king, so I totally understood the allure of Drew. The star football player on a winning football team is everything here, and <i>Battle Baylor</i> is everything there too.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452132102i/17650873._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Naturally Anna assumes Drew is just like every other jock, perhaps even worse since he is the star quarterback. Anna decides her and Drew can hook up, but she won’t offer him anything else, nothing real. To her surprise, Drew proved to be anything, but typical and I fell in love with him. I didn’t love Anna as much, she was much more frustrating since I was so in love with Drew, sigh. However, I didn’t let that deter me since her insecurities were realistic and I can relate. <br><br>This book is super fun, but also had so much heart. I loved that it had both, so few books do.<br><br>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1054412487?book_show_action=true">Sep 14, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="NMmomof4" class="user" itemprop="url" name="NMmomof4" href="/user/show/24665574-nmmomof4">NMmomof4</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1054412487" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6517862104173978445"><b>4.5 Stars <i>(Re-Read 6/29/2018)</i></b><br/><br/><b>4 Stars <i>(Originally Read 9/14/2014)</i></b><br/><br/><b>Overall Opinion: </b> This was another book that I had just left a star rating and not an actual review for, so I decided to give it a re-read. I don't remember it being so deep! We get into these characters on a deeper level then I'm used to with college athlete books. I think that was a good surprise! I love their dialogue. I also love how deeply they cared for and knew each other. I'm increasing my rating from 4 stars to 4.5, because</span>
  <span id="freeText6517862104173978445" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars <i>(Re-Read 6/29/2018)</i></b><br /><br /><b>4 Stars <i>(Originally Read 9/14/2014)</i></b><br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b> This was another book that I had just left a star rating and not an actual review for, so I decided to give it a re-read. I don't remember it being so deep! We get into these characters on a deeper level then I'm used to with college athlete books. I think that was a good surprise! I love their dialogue. I also love how deeply they cared for and knew each other. I'm increasing my rating from 4 stars to 4.5, because I was emotionally invested enough to cry a few times -- and the fact that I've already read this tells me that it's simply <i>that</i> good! I'm still frustrated with the ending, but you know -- blah blah needs a farther glimpse into the future blah blah -- can you tell I'm tired of writing this?! 🙄...Maybe I just need to expect less with endings or something since I'm writing this complaint so much lately 😕🤷🏻‍♀️<br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Anna and Drew's story. They meet in a class their senior year of college. Drew is the star quarterback for the college team, and Anna is not interested in jocks. Drew is instantly interested and starts a strong pursuit of Anna that results in a hook-up. Anna isn't interested in being in the limelight by dating the football player, so she convinces him to keep it casual and not a relationship even though Drew wants it all. There are some funny moments, some hot sexy times, some sad scenes...and they get a HFN ending.<br /><br /><b>POV:</b> This alternated between Anna and Drew's POV.<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Good. It's on the longer side, but I thought it flowed well and I never skimmed.<br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b> Not in the usual way. It takes a while for the h to develop stronger feelings, but the H feels strongly right away (doesn't express love or anything until way later).<br /><br /><b>H rating:</b> 4 stars. Drew. I liked him. I appreciated how he pursued the h. He was also pretty hot!<br /><br /><b>h rating:</b> 4 stars. Anna. I liked her. She was sassy, smart, and I liked how she came to care for the H.<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b>Low/moderate. I did shed a few tears, but I never needed any tissues.<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ They both push away and also pursue the relationship at times, but I'd say that the H is the main pursuer.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Hot. They have some hot tension, chemistry, and scenes -- but not so much it takes away from the story.<br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Yes<br /><br /><b>OW/OM drama:</b> Yes, but when separated <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Both of them see each other out on dates with other people when separated, and this causes jealousy for both of them.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> No<br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b> No<br /><br /><b>Separation:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They are separated for maybe a couple months. They both go on dates with other people, and the H gets kissed by OW (farthest either of them go physically with other people)  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Child abandonment (h's dad - off page), and loss of parents to an accident (H - off page).  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b> This has not enough closure for me. I wanted more! Shocking for me, right?! 😜 I would call this a HFN ending, but others might consider it a HEA <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[they're engaged and living together <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> This one should be either <u>Safe</u> or <u>Safe with exception</u> for most safety gang readers depending on personal preferences.<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have cheating<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a descriptive sex scene with OW/OM<br />- <b> Does</b> have both the h and H pushing away<br />- <b> Does</b> have a separation between the h and H<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have abuse<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a HEA ending <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1056936401" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11644609771812636916"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408658i/799615._SX540_.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>♥♥♥ 4.5 STARS ♥♥♥</b><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425707578i/13919181._SY540_.png' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>“Why won't you let me kiss you, Anna? Why, Anna?"<br/><br/>"It's too much," I rasp.<br/><br/>"Not when I want everything." He says it so deep and strong, a staking of a claim. "And I want everything with you, Anna.” <br/><br/>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410811764i/11155494._SX540_.png' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This was another New Adult winner for me. I really enjoyed this a lot!<br/><br/>Drew "Battle Baylor" is the star quarterback of his team. With the title, comes the unavoidable fame and atte</span>
  <span id="freeText11644609771812636916" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408658i/799615._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>♥♥♥ 4.5 STARS ♥♥♥</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425707578i/13919181._SY540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“Why won't you let me kiss you, Anna? Why, Anna?"<br><br>"It's too much," I rasp.<br><br>"Not when I want everything." He says it so deep and strong, a staking of a claim. "And I want everything with you, Anna.” <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410811764i/11155494._SX540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This was another New Adult winner for me. I really enjoyed this a lot!<br><br>Drew "Battle Baylor" is the star quarterback of his team. With the title, comes the unavoidable fame and attention. As a result, woman fawn over him. A life changing meeting with Anna, has him wanting for the first time ever to pursue someone to have something serious. Unfortunately, Anna doesn't have serious on her mind. She wants him to be a hook up and nothing more. Drew has other plans, and won't give up until he makes Anna his.<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425708005ra/13919344.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“I think you’re beautiful,” he says softly.<br><br>“Beauty fades,” I choke out.<br><br>“Not when it comes from inside.” <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>Oh, Drew...he was super swoony! I really loved him. For a guy that had everything and everyone at his disposal, he was quite down to earth. Sure, at times he could be a bit arrogant but in a very sexy way. I loved the relationship he shared with his teammates. What I loved the most was seeing him try to sway Anna into being in a relationship with him the was more than just sex. He could be so sweet and so caring. He was also very hot, sexy, and alpha.<br><br>Anna, I kind of liked at first. She has gone through some things that make her quite insecure about why on earth a guy like Drew could want her. This insecurity is what caused me to not like her so much. She was just so stubborn and it frustrated me that she kept trying to keep Drew as arm's length emotionally. Then at the end, I liked her again because I liked that she finally did something good. She challenged and cared Drew when he needed it the most. It was so beautiful watching these too interact, especially during those sweet moments that melted my heart.<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425708005ra/13919345.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“Anna, baby, you would never be the girl I didn't see, whether we had met now or in high school." He pulls me in close, rubbing his nose along the tip of mine. "Don't <i>you</i> understand? I know you wouldn't be because, since the moment I laid eyes on you, you're all I <i>can</i> see.” <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>The story overall, was very good, and romantic. There wasn't any over the top drama that dragged things out. There was some angst in this book but it was a good amount. It wasn't all the color of roses as there were some intense moments between the main characters that tugged at my heart strings. I couldn't put this book down because I loved all of those emotional scenes. I really did like this book, and it's definitely one I would recommend you give a read. Especially to those who love the New Adult genre. I can't wait to see what is next in the series.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410811764i/11155494._SX540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1138236815" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9441520901551226971"><b>
  <i>***4 "Big Red" stars for Baylor and Jones***</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449162473i/17243940.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I really don't know how to start this review... I feel i'm in loss of pretty words and it's difficult for me to describe the situation that Drew and Anna caught themselves up!!<br/>This was a very nice story that made me pass from many stages while i was reading it...<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449162474ra/17243941.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/>I had heard so many good words about this book and i wanted so badly to read it, but at the same time something was holding me back and then one day i decided that it was about time...<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449162474ra/17243942.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>And </span>
  <span id="freeText9441520901551226971" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>***4 "Big Red" stars for Baylor and Jones***</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449162473i/17243940.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I really don't know how to start this review... I feel i'm in loss of pretty words and it's difficult for me to describe the situation that Drew and Anna caught themselves up!!<br>This was a very nice story that made me pass from many stages while i was reading it...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449162474ra/17243941.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>I had heard so many good words about this book and i wanted so badly to read it, but at the same time something was holding me back and then one day i decided that it was about time...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449162474ra/17243942.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And i started it!!! And i felt rush and excitement and then i started to feel annoyance toward Anna... and so much sympathy for Drew...<br>And the annoyance continued because Anna was so damn stubborn and i wanted to shake her up to open her eyes and see the truth that was lying inside her heart...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409200ra/801130.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>But Anna and Drew made it a fuckin' mess and i was with Drew's side...<br><i>(Okay that's an understatement because i was almost all the time with Drew's side!!! Soooorry, Anna!!!)</i><br>And God, something bad happened and finally followed something good and i felt relief and almost happiness, but then for first time Drew disappointed me!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449162474ra/17243943.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>But after all those shit that i had to get through, everything went good!!! Thank God!!!<br><br>As you can understand those two were so fuckin' messed up, but who isn't???<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1404257532ra/10215587.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>But i will have to admit that this story was feeling like reality!!! <br>It wasn't something extraordinary that nobody from all of us wouldn't do...<br>And i like that!!!<br>Drew and Anna were two normal people with their fears, their insecurities, they ups and their downs, with dark days and beautiful days, with sex and snuggling, with fights and overeacting...<br>In many points it reminded me of myself... <br>And i liked that it seemed so real...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449162474ra/17243944.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I won't tell you much about the story.<br>Drew was the star of the campus, he liked Anna and he went after her.<br>Anna had her issues, she had a bad opinion of Drew and she didn't want anything more than a hook-up...<br>They hooked up but Drew was insisting for more, but Anna wasn't agree. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444477252ra/16506832.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>So, they made this deal... they gonna only hooking up... <br>Anna preffered to refuse her feelings and she even refused her kisses to Drew because this action was too intimate.<br>And Drew fell hard for Anna and he was tiptoying around her from the fear to lose what little she was giving to him.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449162474ra/17243945.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>You think that this deal could be successfull??? Or everything will go to hell???</i><br>I can't tell you more... so you have to find all about their relationship by yourselves!!!<br><br><b>
  <i>"She didn’t even let me kiss her. That burns the most. As if kissing me was so personal that she couldn’t bear it. As if she needed to relegate me to some random, near faceless fuck...<br>I’ve just experienced the hottest, most erotic, life-changing sex of my life, and I don’t think I’m going to get a repeat. Tonight was obviously an ill-advised hook up for her. And I’m so screwed because it was the best thing that has ever happened to me."</i>
</b><br><br>Drew "Battle" Baylor seemed like the usual stereotypical joke, but he was far away from that role.<br>I saw a sweet and caring man and i couldn't do anything than sympathize him. He was a very good man.<br>And he had true feelings for Anna. But she was hurting him with her attitude and i was furious for her behalf.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449162474ra/17243946.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>Who wouldn't want a man like him around her??? Not me, for sure!!!<br>I wanted to punch Anna for the insecurity that she was causing him!!! He didn't deserve to get through all those shits that she was throwing to his way.<br>But to be fair, near to the end, he made me mad too!!! <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1409085834ra/10932036.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>He was a little bit irrational, but i forgive him!!!<br>He deserved for once to be the one who was a little bit... off!!!<br><br><b>
  <i>“You’ve destroyed me, Anna Jones.”<br>I know exactly what he means, because he’s destroyed me too."</i>
</b><br><br>As for Anna Jones??? I have to admit that in the most part of the book, she was irritating me very much.<br>I know that she was having feelings for Drew from the first moment, but this denial was driving me crazy and it was hurting Drew!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449162474ra/17243947.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Yep, at some point i understood her reasons for all this insecurity and attitude but i think that Drew never gave her the opportunity to doubt his feelings.<br>So, she was unfair to him and i didn't like that! <br>They could be so perfect together from the first moment, but she didn't aloud it!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449162474ra/17243948.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"An insidious voice in my head shouts Danger, I’d Turn Back If I Were You! This is too close to a relationship. I don’t want one. Not with him.<br>The worst part is, I’m lying to myself. He isn’t the arrogant jerk I thought he was. I want him. Constantly."</i>
</b><br><br>But at the last 60 pages, i really liked that woman... She stood by her man's side and she fought for him...<br>I really liked how she stood to Drew at their biggest fight. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449162474ra/17243949.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I admired her for that and for some other things before that...<br><br>Drew and Anna were having great chemistry and when they were together everything was smooth and beautiful...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449162624ra/17243957.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>When they were apart everything was dark and meaningless.<br>And that's why i was mad with them... <i>For the lost time...</i><br><br><b>
  <i>“You’re my home, Drew.”<br>“We’ll be each other’s home.”</i>
</b><br><br>I will admit that Gray Grayson intrigued me a lot and now i can't wait to see what is his deal!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449162474ra/17243951.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>He was funny and a little bit meathead, but i really liked how close he was with Drew and how he was handling all the bullshits that Drew pulled out at him near to the end!!!<br>I can't wait for his turn!!!<br><br><b>
  <i>“What’s the matter? Red didn’t respond to the ‘Battle’ cry?”<br>“Fuck off, Gray.” </i>
</b><br><i>(Bahahaha.... That was very funny!!!)</i></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8346712882640739943">Find all of my reviews at: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/'>http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/</a><br/><br/>Drew Baylor is the star quarterback for the football team who has a reputation for being a player both on and off the field. Anna Jones is a curvy girl-next-door type who has <b>zero</b> interest being another notch on Baylor’s bedpost. You know what that means, right?<br/><br/><a href='http://lunapic.com' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462290595ra/18977824.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I noticed <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1620253186?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>Mrs. Joseph</a> reading another book in this series and it peaked my interest because of . . . <br/><br/><a href='http://lunapic.com' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462290595ra/18977825.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Mmmmmmmm, beard. Unfortunately the porny liburry did not have that o</span>
  <span id="freeText8346712882640739943" style="display:none">Find all of my reviews at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/">http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/</a><br><br>Drew Baylor is the star quarterback for the football team who has a reputation for being a player both on and off the field. Anna Jones is a curvy girl-next-door type who has <b>zero</b> interest being another notch on Baylor’s bedpost. You know what that means, right?<br><br><a href="http://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462290595ra/18977824.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I noticed <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1620253186?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Mrs. Joseph</a> reading another book in this series and it peaked my interest because of . . . <br><br><a href="http://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462290595ra/18977825.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Mmmmmmmm, beard. Unfortunately the porny liburry did not have that one available on Kindle so I had to settle for this one instead. Allow me a moment to go off the rails here (so unusual for me, I know). Praise Jeebus the library had THIS cover . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462290595i/18977827.jpg" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Because <b>YUM</b> and I’ll take that with cheese. If the alternate cover would have been my option . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462290595i/18977826.jpg" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I probably would have skipped it. I don’t want to make the sexy with that guy. Just a note to authors that books are indeed judged by their covers. Especially pornos. You have two options – abtastic with an “accessory” (a football, motorcycle, tattoos, beard, whatevs) or “I wanna bang that tiger in the hoodie” like such . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462290595i/18977828.jpg" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I really need to buy that book. Alright, enough of that. Let’s get back on track – or as much on track as is possible for me. So Caleb and Anna meet in philosophy class or some crap that I can’t be bothered to remember because really I just read these for . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462290595ra/18977829.gif" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>#sploosh.<br><br>His reputation proceeds him, she has body issues and whatever that she seriously needs to work out because damn girl high school ended quite some time ago and no one ever bothered you at college until you started banging superstud because DUH jealous hos. However, lucky for us readers they see each other at a party and both have an itch that needs scratching so you know what that means . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462290595i/18977830._SX540_.jpg" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And let me tell you, those bathroom sexytimes were H.O.T. Whoooooooooo doggy . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462290595ra/18977831.gif" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Of course, this being NA there had to be that little thing that gets in the way called an attempt at a plot. While Drew (did I call him Caleb somewhere because I seriously keep wanting to type Caleb and I’m not even gonna go check myself) and Anna quickly realize that much like the Usher song, they got it they got it bad . . . <br><br><a href="http://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462290595ra/18977832.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>(#droooooool #homersimpsonnoise)<br><br>It is not without angst and manufactured drama that is supposed to make you all . . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462290595ra/18977833.gif" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But instead makes me more like this . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462290595ra/18977834.gif" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>The Game Plan</i> could have earned 4 Stars, but I’m sticking with three because seriously enough is e-mothereffing-nuff with the drama llama and this could have <b>easily</b> been a hundred pages shorter and wrapped up without me getting stabby.</span>

<div id="review_1052773849" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1052773849" />
    <a title="Eda**" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6285155-eda"><img alt="Eda**" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1581410351p2/6285155.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1052773849?book_show_action=true">Sep 12, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Eda**" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Eda**" href="/user/show/6285155-eda">Eda**</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6285155-eda?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1052773849" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10234883121081362112"><br/><b>
  <i>** 5++ "<u>My world lives in your palm, Anna</u>" STARS **</i>
</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You've destroyed me, Anna Jones."<br/>~ DREW</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393681ra/758009.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Such a beautiful story...<br/><br/><i>GOD,</i> I'm so glad I picked this one up after resisting it for so damn long. Once again, I am reminded of the stupidity of prejudice. I normally try to refrain from NA Romance, because they're mostly...well, the same sh*t with slight subject differences.<br/><br/>But this one was <b>
  <u>GOLDEN</u>
</b>. Somehow I felt totally sucked into the story and had to abandon all my earthly responsi</span>
  <span id="freeText10234883121081362112" style="display:none"><br><b>
  <i>** 5++ "<u>My world lives in your palm, Anna</u>" STARS **</i>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You've destroyed me, Anna Jones."<br>~ DREW</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393681ra/758009.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Such a beautiful story...<br><br><i>GOD,</i> I'm so glad I picked this one up after resisting it for so damn long. Once again, I am reminded of the stupidity of prejudice. I normally try to refrain from NA Romance, because they're mostly...well, the same sh*t with slight subject differences.<br><br>But this one was <b>
  <u>GOLDEN</u>
</b>. Somehow I felt totally sucked into the story and had to abandon all my earthly responsibilities to see how this messy little love story wraps up, anxious to get to the next page.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1402018625ra/9883255.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>When <u>Anna Jones</u> hurried to take her seat in the classroom after being a bit late, how could she have known that the king of college football and the boy coloring every damn girl’s dreams on campus, <u>Drew Baylor</u>, would sit right next to her? <i>And that’s not even the good part:</i> After the minute their eyes meet, Drew never takes his away from her, staring at her with lusty eyes and acting all awestruck and sh*t!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412951238ra/11446655.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Anna feels a pull like she has never experienced before. She wants to jump onto this guy’s lap and cling to him like a koala…<i>
  <b>until he opens his mouth and starts speaking, that is.</b>
</i><br><br>Drew knows the second the words <i>“Big Red”</i> leave his lips that he has colossally f*cked up. After all, they’re not the best words to use for a curvy redhead like Anna. And Anna is not exactly as calm and quiet as she seems, apparently, because she immediately gives Drew a piece of her mind for the ridiculous nickname. <i>What a first impression, right?</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385792923ra/7229078.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Anna wants nothing to do with Drew. He’s not her type anyway. She is into the emotional and poetic guys, not the popular playboys with cocky grins. So what if she can’t get him out of her mind and that she gets all hot and bothered when he is near? He is definitely not good for her, so she tries to avoid Drew like the plague. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/642019.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But Drew is goddamn stubborn and will not give up till he gets Anna. <b>All of her.</b> He is used to girls throwing themselves at his feet, but not Anna. No, she acts like she couldn't care less about him. For the first time in his life, he actually has to work for it.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412951238ra/11446656.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When these two finally give in to their desires, it’s the best sexual experience either one has ever had. Now that they have tasted from the forbidden fruit, they want more and they will never be able to get enough, it seems.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412951238ra/11446657.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>Anna is terrified though. She has never been the center of attention of any boy before. She was a shadow and a subject of jokes in high school. She was the girl that no one even noticed, except for the times that she was bullied. She doesn't believe that someone like Drew can ever care for her. She has to protect herself. But she can’t stop herself from wanting him either, so she comes up with rules for their “relationship”: <u>
  <b>No kissing on the mouth, no staying for the night, no telling anyone and no falling in love.</b>
</u><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I've just experienced the hottest, most erotic, life-changing sex of my life and I don't think I'm going to get a repeat. Tonight was obviously an ill-advised hook up for her. And I'm screwed because it was the best thing that has ever happened to me.<br>~ DREW</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Drew wants more. He wants everything with Anna. <i>And he will get it…</i> He just has to be patient and prove to her that he is not the Drew that everyone else sees. He has to prove that he can be the right guy for her.<br><br>Will Drew manage to open Anna’s eyes to see the love emanating from his? Will Anna be courageous enough to trust Drew and give him her heart in exchange for his? It’s a battle of insecurities and trust. Let’s see which gets to come out the winner.<br><br><b>
  <u>GAME ON!</u>
</b><br><br>Drew was perfection. His tough exterior combined with the interior vulnerability and loneliness just stole my breath away. His determination to persuade Anna, despite her mistakes and bad choices and his heartbreak when he gets rejected, just made my heart melt. His charming ways were the best thing about this book.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I want her here forever. I'm twenty-three years old, my carefully built life has just been smashed to pieces, yet I know with complete clarity that I never want to be parted from Anna Jones.<br>~ DREW</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You have my heart, Anna. And every time I had to walk away from you, every time you walked away from me, it felt like it was being ripped out of my chest. It f*cking hurt, Anna."<br>~ DREW</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412951238ra/11446658.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>At times, I wanted to smash Anna’s face into a glass and scream at her for being a complete fool. I didn't exactly like her for most of the book, but that changed once she didn't give up on Drew when he started making huge mistakes because of the stinky mood he was in. She stood up for herself, for Drew, for their love. I adored that about her and she instantly won my heart.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412951238ra/11446659.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I’d like to add that the interaction between Drew and his teammates was also a good reason for me to fall for this book. All the guys were adorable and interesting and so much fun! I can’t wait to read the stories of each and every one of them! Gray is up next and I simply can’t wait!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381429752ra/4848600.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is a story full of emotion and angst but there is no exaggerated and pointless drama, which makes it perfect and puts it into a separate shelf from other NA Romance books for me.<br><br>I recommend it to <b>EVERYONE</b> that likes to read a sweet but sexy-as-hell romantic story!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I thought I had lost myself in Drew. But the truth was that I'd found myself in him.<br>~ ANNA</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412951969ra/11446776.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="10234883121081362112" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1442998942" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1442998942" />
    <a title="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10336538-jessica-silverbow"><img alt="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1393785730p2/10336538.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1442998942?book_show_action=true">Nov 15, 2015</a>

<div id="review_1244789526" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1244789526" />
    <a title="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover"><img alt="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1489089790p2/34338862.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1244789526?book_show_action=true">Apr 03, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" class="user" itemprop="url" name="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" href="/user/show/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover">TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/24852488-the-hook-up">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover?shelf=let-me-have-your-babies">let-me-have-your-babies</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1244789526" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1896779970608742389"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446411846i/16803063._SY540_.jpg' width='450' height='450' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>In a world of stories with predictable plot twists, characters with haunted pasts, and unnecessary shock value thrown in for good measure, I personally have found it SO HARD to find a light read that isn’t beyond cheesy or just….well, boring.<br/><br/>So when one comes along with one of the most fantastic heroes I have read about, I want to scream “YES FINALLY!!!!!” from the top of my lungs.<br/><br/>Basic plot - Drew is Mr. Popular Star Quarterback of his college, and Anna catches his eye on their first day of cl</span>
  <span id="freeText1896779970608742389" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446411846i/16803063._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>In a world of stories with predictable plot twists, characters with haunted pasts, and unnecessary shock value thrown in for good measure, I personally have found it SO HARD to find a light read that isn’t beyond cheesy or just….well, boring.<br><br>So when one comes along with one of the most fantastic heroes I have read about, I want to scream “YES FINALLY!!!!!” from the top of my lungs.<br><br>Basic plot - Drew is Mr. Popular Star Quarterback of his college, and Anna catches his eye on their first day of class. While Drew is sweet, charismatic, and confident, Anna has some insecurities and can’t seem to understand why Drew would want her. They hook up, but Anna tries to keep Drew at a distance for fear of being consumed by her attraction to him and getting her heart broken.<br><br>I must admit, the beginning of The Hook Up had me feeling a tad iffy. I am not a fan of insta-love, and can count on one hand the amount of times I have read it and felt it was actually believable or without making me want to roll my eyes. When Anna and Drew meet that ‘insta-connection’ was there, but I was able to look past it because I found Drew’s opening lines humorous and his endearing charm just reeled me in.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446411846i/16803064._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>
  <u>Without a doubt, Drew is what undeniably made this book. He is absolute PERFECTION.</u>
</b> I cannot stress enough how much I adored his character. He was everything you could ask for in a hero. Sweet, SEXY AS ALL FREAKING HELL, patient, understanding….I can go on and on. With his amazing character and Kristen Callihan’s FANTASTIC writing, I was definitely hooked. I haven’t read anything by this author before, and was pleasantly surprised with how smooth, witty, and touching her writing was. I’ve said it before and I’ll say it again. Dialogue is what makes or breaks a book for me. The conversations, texts, and ESPECIALLY the romantic lines in here were GOLD. I must have highlighted every word that came out of Drew’s delicious mouth.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446411846i/16803065._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I would also like to point out, while I am a fan of <i>the dirty talk</i>, I found it so refreshing to have a male character who didn’t spew one liners the whole time they were having sex. Nope, not Drew *le sighhhh*. Their chemistry was so off the freaking charts HOT words weren’t really needed. Instead, Drew would dish out one sexy ass command and BOOM, there went Anna’s panties. And mine. I honestly feel like writing a good sex scene takes talent and I LOVEEEDDD how Kristen handled and wrote them. They were so steamy but at the same time so emotionally charged. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446411846i/16803066._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>
  <i>I Should Note</i>
</b>…. Though I tried to understand Anna’s feelings, I kept going back and forth between being annoyed and sympathizing with her. By the time we got a deeper look into her insecurities, though, the annoyance waned. I’ve never understood or been a fan of the whole “you can fuck me but we can’t try anything more” and “even though we’re fucking and you shower me with love and attention, I’m still going to be a snot because I think you’ll hurt me” bit. And because Drew made it SO obviously clear he adored Anna and was nothing short of amazing it made it hard for me to understand her reluctance. It would have been easier to sympathize with her more if he was a known jerk or player with a seedy past, but Drew was someone anyone and everyone would pine for. He’s THAT amazing. BUT (and this is a pretty big BUT) Anna most definitely earned back points towards the end of the book. I grew to like her so much more as the book progressed. I also really would have loved more chapters in Drew's POV. But mainly because I just couldn’t get enough of him.<br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446411846i/16803067._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>All in all, I enjoyed this read SO MUCH and have found a new book BF in Drew. <b>
  <i>I am utterly obsessed with this boy.</i>
</b> I would highly recommend this to others, especially if you’ve been having a hard time finding entertaining books that aren’t predictable and cheesy. The story got better and better with each page. I really loved Drew and Gray’s friendship so I will definitely be continuing with this series and am excited to get to know Gray in the next book!<br><br><a href="https://thecrazyworldofabooklover.wordpress.com/" target="blog" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467902722i/19644381._SX540_.jpg" width="275" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>Find Me On:<br><a href="https://www.instagram.com/thecrazyworldofabooklover/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> ❤ <a href="https://www.facebook.com/profile.php?id=100009277089211" rel="nofollow noopener">FB Page</a> ❤ <a href="https://www.facebook.com/TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover/" rel="nofollow noopener">FB Blog</a> ❤ <a href="https://thecrazyworldofabooklover.wordpress.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="1896779970608742389" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1044792348" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1044792348" />
    <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts"><img alt="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1378340325p2/17755575.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1044792348?book_show_action=true">Sep 03, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts">Wendy&#39;sThoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23171970-the-hook-up">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText"> Kristen Callihan Fans, Romance</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Wendy'sThoughts by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/6082482-didi">Didi</a>
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1044792348" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3746322321039998363"><b>5 Seeing Who You Are Through Eyes Others Stars <br/>* * * * * <i>Spoiler Free</i><br/>Learning who we are is such a challenge. We experience so much during our formative years and how we see ourselves from that time can leave a scar so deep...it can skew our perceptions emotionally. <br/><br/>We may know we lost all the awkwardness or weight from early school years... we may know we are capable, smart and independent. We may also know we don't fit into the stereotypes of what our "place" is but emotionally... hat is so mu</b></span>
  <span id="freeText3746322321039998363" style="display:none"><b>5 Seeing Who You Are Through Eyes Others Stars <br>* * * * * <i>Spoiler Free</i><br>Learning who we are is such a challenge. We experience so much during our formative years and how we see ourselves from that time can leave a scar so deep...it can skew our perceptions emotionally. <br><br>We may know we lost all the awkwardness or weight from early school years... we may know we are capable, smart and independent. We may also know we don't fit into the stereotypes of what our "place" is but emotionally... hat is so much harder.<br><br>This is a story that focuses on all of these things with a deft hand and a finely written story. The idea isn't new...it has been done before. But the way we meet the characters and feel for them from the start... and the way we are in their heads sharing with us every step of the way... works so well.</b><br><br>Both characters have much in common; one has lost his parents in an accident when he was almost out of high school. Our fella, Drew, had the support and love of his family for his formative years and gave him life lessons which have held him well. When he experiences a love smack for the first time, startled beyond reason...he has these moments from both his Mother and Father talking him through... guiding him... helping him along the way.<br><br>Because he is going to need all the help he can get with this desire for Anna Jones. She is like no other person he has ever met. She isn't among the legions who drool and follow him around because he is the star quarterback of the football team. She is not like the endless stream of women dying to say they had him because of "who" he is. He has been taken - hook line and sinker because she is a vision; she is smart, quick and keeps him on his mental toes.... and best of all she see him- Drew- for who he is without all the sports stuff around him. <br><br>Anna, though, cannot see why he would be interested in her. She knows she has a curvy body and has come to terms with it. She has the brains and wherewithal to handle her courses and excel. She also knows she is soooo not in his league. It was a lesson taught to her from school, where she wished to hide and disappear...to escape the looks she got because of her budding figure. She learned early men leave and love is fleeting. The lesson taught well from the abandonment of her father at seven. So when her heart starts pumping and she starts to always be aware of Drew whenever he is around... she either has to steel herself from ever crossing that line...or just give in to a hookup and get this crazy notion out of her head.<br><br>This is a story surround by circumstances... senior year of college... the pressure of the football season and future career... and the understanding of what it is like to be so overwhelmed by your heart's wants. These characters are complete for me. They have support systems in friends, coaches, and even through themselves when needed. The growth arcs were handled realistically and though there was the normal NA angst... it was done where we could get it or felt it wasn't too much.<br><br>What also worked so well was the want these two had for each other. Heatwaves surfaced off the pages...need, desperate need we all have felt at a time in our lives was present for us to experience again...it was a thing of beauty for me.<br><br>This is much more than a book about college lovers finding themselves. It was more insightful on so many other levels. It touched off the hypocrisy of Colleges and how they treat athletes. How they turn the other way and do not give them the education they deserve. It touches on what is a home... and how we make our own when we need to, and it touches on accepting who we are and allowing others to really see us and accept us, too.<br><br><i>I found this book through my friend Didi. She did a wonderful review<br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1040896831">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a></i><br><br>and it pushed me to read it sooner rather than later. I thank her for the terrific night and the next day I spent reading this. I highly recommend this and hope you enjoy it as much as I have. The good news is more about this group of friends is coming. I will be looking for its release date :D <br> <br><i>A gifted copy was provided by author/publisher for an honest review.</i><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22611920.The_Hook_Up__Game_On___1_" title="The Hook Up (Game On, #1) by Kristen Callihan" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1407891923l/22611920._SY75_.jpg" alt="The Hook Up (Game On, #1) by Kristen Callihan" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b> The Hook Up (Game On, #1)<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1044792348">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23122175.The_Friend_Zone__Game_On___2_" title="The Friend Zone (Game On, #2) by Kristen Callihan" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1430227184l/23122175._SY75_.jpg" alt="The Friend Zone (Game On, #2) by Kristen Callihan" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a>The Friend Zone (Game On, #2)<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1261709854">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23204215.The_Game_Plan__Game_On___3_" title="The Game Plan (Game On, #3) by Kristen Callihan" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1445605918l/23204215._SY75_.jpg" alt="The Game Plan (Game On, #3) by Kristen Callihan" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> The Game Plan (Game On, #3)<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29541797.The_Hot_Shot__Game_On___4_" title="The Hot Shot (Game On, #4) by Kristen Callihan" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1489760751l/29541797._SY75_.jpg" alt="The Hot Shot (Game On, #4) by Kristen Callihan" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> The Hot Shot (Game On, #4)<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29541805.Untitled__Game_On___5_" title="Untitled (Game On, #5) by Kristen Callihan" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/book/50x75-a91bf249278a81aabab721ef782c4a74.png" alt="Untitled (Game On, #5) by Kristen Callihan" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> Untitled (Game On, #5)<br><br> <br><strong>For more Reviews, Free E-books and Giveaways</strong><br><div>

<div id="review_1272927472" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1272927472" />
    <a title="Laura" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8429172-laura"><img alt="Laura" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595453256p2/8429172.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1272927472?book_show_action=true">May 05, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1272927472" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8751580325721172639">DNF @ 48%<br/><br/>I started this book with a lot of hope. No one I know have rated this book lower than 4 stars! I needed some contemporary romance so enter The Hook Up.<br/><br/>I was not hooked up at all.<br/><br/>I just didn't like the characters. Drew is so obsessed with Anna, it's ridiculous. For the first 20 or so pages he did nothing but describe how perfect she was and how hard she got him all the time even when she openly ignored him. <br/><br/>He was like a brainless dude who could only function with his junk.<br/><br/>And Anna, damn</span>
  <span id="freeText8751580325721172639" style="display:none">DNF @ 48%<br /><br />I started this book with a lot of hope. No one I know have rated this book lower than 4 stars! I needed some contemporary romance so enter The Hook Up.<br /><br />I was not hooked up at all.<br /><br />I just didn't like the characters. Drew is so obsessed with Anna, it's ridiculous. For the first 20 or so pages he did nothing but describe how perfect she was and how hard she got him all the time even when she openly ignored him. <br /><br />He was like a brainless dude who could only function with his junk.<br /><br />And Anna, damn. She's so plain. What's her deal? Nothing.<br /><br />Nothing was her deal.<br /><br />She was just there. Existing. Being Drew's object of desire. That's it.<br /><br />I wasn't fan of the writing style, the story was full of cliches and I just didn't care for the characters. <br /><br />I can tell y'all how this book ends and who are in the next ones because that's how predictable this story was.<br /><br />*Guy and girl meet, instant connection<br />*Guy lusts after girl, girl tries to resist because "she's better than that"<br />*Guy doesn't take a no for an answer <br />*Girl says no when she wants to say yes<br />*Mean girls (fucking stop this already)<br /><br />I could go on and on but this book bored me to death.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8751580325721172639" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
